Sign in to edit
  • History

Script from King's Quest Chapter I: A Knight to Remember. This may be missing some narrative, including voiceovers that don't don't have subtitles or the conversation between Manny and Achaka.

The transcript can be found in the files and opened with a standard word document program (in the Folder: GrahamsGame/Localizatio/INT).

Whisper's Stories[]

Story A[]

Whisper: At last the ivory monster unveiled itself. It bared its teeth in a grin wider than my arms could stretch. My heart stopped. An ear piercing screech woke me from my daze, and I dove behind cover. It clawed its way towards me howling as it tore into the others around me. I wasn't sure if I was going to make it. A voice rang out across the hushed forest, its only words echoed through the barked masses. Do you whisper? In that moment knew, I did. I cried out, I do, I do want to live, and with that I dashed past the lunging grasp of the monster's maids and minions and found I was incredibly fast. Why, it was quite unbelievable, but not totally, right?

RG1: Oh no, that was amazing, and you lived to tell the tale.

Whisper: Yes it is me, standing before you.

RG2: I can't just even, I would have been so scared.

Whisper: Many are, many freeze. But for me, well, I never freeze.

Story B[]

Whisper: I had nearly unearthed the treasure that was within. I could feel the riches at the edges of my fingertips when it clasped shut. My arm was pinched between the treasure and its casing. I couldn't stay, if I did I would lose circulation and my limb would be lost. If I tried to remove my arm, it would be sliced from wrist to elbow. I didn't have much time, and then a sharp snort erupted through the shadows. It heard me, there were no options. If that treasure was to be mine, I had to sacrifice my arm for the good of the rest of me. I flung my pinched arm downward as hard as I could. The treasure shook inside, but my arm remained. Foorsteps, no time to run, no time to thin, only action. I jumped off the wall and fell into a deep pit. A crash, treasure everywhere. A yawn behind me, it was awoken. I scrambled to grab each piece and hurled one into the darkness. Grahaharrr (sp?)! It called out into pain, as I heard its body crash to the floor. Treasure in hand, I escaped, and ventured onward.

RG1: Oh how delightful, and you escaped with all the treasure!

Whisper: Yes, I relished every last bit of that treasure.

Story C[]

Whisper: The flames danced right before my eyes I couldn't go anywhere, they had me surrounded. I watched the flames grow, each ember reaching closer to my face. Then I knew, there was a way out. I blew as hard as I could, countering that incendiary torturing device, and extinguished each and every flame. The horde inched towards me, their cult like call ringing through my ears. I leapt up and kicked one square in the throat, silencing his off pitched blathering. The others shocked by this sight silenced themselves and bowed down to the hero you see, standing in front of you.

RG1: What a happy avenger!

Whisper: It seems I tell this legend every year.

RG2: Ahh, how can I be you?

Story D[]

Whisper: There was no looking past it. Every corner of my peripheral, he was there awaiting to be acknowledged. Stalwartly mocking me, there he stood the largest beast I had ever seen. He called to me, staring me down right between my eyes. I raised my hands every so slightly to ready myself, but I twitched only for an instant, and he saw it. He gathered his troops and fortified his walls. We wrestled for days squeezing the life from each other's souls. When we both could take no more, I somehow found the strength. Your hero mustered up everything inside of him, and pushed that beast over the edge. The beast's guts exploded everywhere, and I was left with a mess...

RG1: How do you do it?

Whisper: What can I say, adventure just bursts through my skin.
